4528/* Definitions used in the body of the `gconv' function. */
4529#define CHARSET_NAME "CP932//"
4530#define FROM_LOOP from_cp932
4531#define TO_LOOP to_cp932
4532#define DEFINE_INIT 1
4533#define DEFINE_FINI 1
4534#define MIN_NEEDED_FROM 1
4535#define MAX_NEEDED_FROM 2
4536#define MIN_NEEDED_TO 4
4537#define ONE_DIRECTION 0
4538
4539/* First define the conversion function from CP932 to UCS4. */
4540#define MIN_NEEDED_INPUT MIN_NEEDED_FROM
4541#define MAX_NEEDED_INPUT MAX_NEEDED_FROM
4542#define MIN_NEEDED_OUTPUT MIN_NEEDED_TO
4543#define LOOPFCT FROM_LOOP
4544#define BODY \
4545 { \
4546 uint32_t ch = *inptr; \
4547 \
4548 if (ch < 0x80) \
4549 ++inptr; \
4550 else if (ch >= 0xa1 && ch <= 0xdf) \
4551 { \
4552 ch += 0xfec0; \
4553 ++inptr; \
4554 } \
4555 else if (__builtin_expect (ch, 0) == 0xa0 \
4556 || __builtin_expect (ch <= 0x80, 0) \
4557 || __builtin_expect (ch > 0xfc, 0)) \
4558 { \
4559 /* These are illegal. */ \
4560 if (! ignore_errors_p ()) \
4561 { \
4562 /* This is an illegal character. */ \
4563 result = __GCONV_ILLEGAL_INPUT; \
4564 break; \
4565 } \
4566 \
4567 ++inptr; \
4568 ++*irreversible; \
4569 continue; \
4570 } \
4571 else \
4572 { \
4573 /* Two-byte character. First test whether the next character \
4574 is also available. */ \
4575 uint32_t ch2; \
4576 uint_fast32_t idx; \
4577 \
4578 if (__glibc_unlikely (inptr + 1 >= inend)) \
4579 { \
4580 /* The second character is not available. Store \
4581 the intermediate result. */ \
4582 result = __GCONV_INCOMPLETE_INPUT; \
4583 break; \
4584 } \
4585 \
4586 ch2 = inptr[1]; \
4587 idx = ch * 256 + ch2; \
4588 if (__builtin_expect (ch2 < 0x40, 0) \
4589 || __builtin_expect (ch2 > 0xfc, 0) \
4590 || __builtin_expect (ch2 == 0x7f, 0) \
4591 || (__builtin_expect (idx > 0x84be, 0) && idx < 0x8740) \
4592 || (__builtin_expect (idx > 0x879c, 0) && idx < 0x889f) \
4593 || (__builtin_expect (idx > 0x88fc, 0) && idx < 0x8940) \
4594 || (__builtin_expect (idx > 0x9ffc, 0) && idx < 0xe040) \
4595 || (__builtin_expect (idx > 0xeaa4, 0) && idx < 0xed40) \
4596 || (__builtin_expect (idx > 0xeefc, 0) && idx < 0xf040) \
4597 || __builtin_expect (idx > 0xfc4b, 0)) \
4598 { \
4599 /* This is illegal. */ \
4600 if (! ignore_errors_p ()) \
4601 { \
4602 /* This is an illegal character. */ \
4603 result = __GCONV_ILLEGAL_INPUT; \
4604 break; \
4605 } \
4606 \
4607 ++inptr; \
4608 ++*irreversible; \
4609 continue; \
4610 } \
4611 \
4612 /* We could pack the data a bit more dense. The second \
4613 byte will never be 0x7f and it will also be never \
4614 >0xfc. But this would mean yet more `if's. */ \
4615 if (idx <= 0x84be) \
4616 ch = cjk_block1[(ch - 0x81) * 192 + ch2 - 0x40]; \
4617 else if (idx <= 0x879c) \
4618 ch = cjk_block2[(ch - 0x87) * 192 + ch2 - 0x40]; \
4619 else if (idx <= 0x88fc) \
4620 ch = cjk_block3[(ch - 0x88) * 192 + ch2 - 0x9f]; \
4621 else if (idx <= 0x9ffc) \
4622 ch = cjk_block4[(ch - 0x89) * 192 + ch2 - 0x40]; \
4623 else if (idx <= 0xeaa4) \
4624 ch = cjk_block5[(ch - 0xe0) * 192 + ch2 - 0x40]; \
4625 else if (idx <= 0xeefc) \
4626 ch = cjk_block6[(ch - 0xed) * 192 + ch2 - 0x40]; \
4627 else if (idx <= 0xf9fc) \
4628 ch = (ch-0xf0)*188 + ch2-((ch2<0x7f)?0x40:0x41) + 0xe000; \
4629 else \
4630 ch = cjk_block7[(ch - 0xfa) * 192 + ch2 - 0x40]; \
4631 \
4632 if (__builtin_expect (ch, 1) == 0) \
4633 { \
4634 /* This is an illegal character. */ \
4635 if (! ignore_errors_p ()) \
4636 { \
4637 /* This is an illegal character. */ \
4638 result = __GCONV_ILLEGAL_INPUT; \
4639 break; \
4640 } \
4641 \
4642 inptr += 2; \
4643 ++*irreversible; \
4644 continue; \
4645 } \
4646 \
4647 inptr += 2; \
4648 } \
4649 \
4650 put32 (outptr, ch); \
4651 outptr += 4; \
4652 }
4653#define LOOP_NEED_FLAGS
4654#include <iconv/loop.c>
4655
4656
4657/* Next, define the other direction. */
4658#define MIN_NEEDED_INPUT MIN_NEEDED_TO
4659#define MIN_NEEDED_OUTPUT MIN_NEEDED_FROM
4660#define MAX_NEEDED_OUTPUT MAX_NEEDED_FROM
4661#define LOOPFCT TO_LOOP
4662#define BODY \
4663 { \
4664 uint32_t ch = get32 (inptr); \
4665 const char *cp; \
4666 unsigned char pua[2]; \
4667 \
4668 if (ch >= (sizeof (from_ucs4_lat1) / sizeof (from_ucs4_lat1[0]))) \
4669 { \
4670 if (ch >= 0x0391 && ch <= 0x0451) \
4671 cp = from_ucs4_greek[ch - 0x391]; \
4672 else if (ch >= 0x2010 && ch <= 0x9fa0) \
4673 cp = from_ucs4_cjk[ch - 0x2010]; \
4674 else if (ch >= 0xe000 && ch <= 0xe757) \
4675 { \
4676 pua[0] = (ch - 0xe000) / 188 + 0xf0; \
4677 pua[1] = (ch - 0xe000) % 188 + 0x40; \
4678 if (pua[1] > 0x7e) \
4679 pua[1]++; \
4680 cp = (const char *)&(pua[0]); \
4681 } \
4682 else if (ch >= 0xf929 && ch <= 0xfa2d) \
4683 cp = from_ucs4_cjkcpt[ch - 0xf929]; \
4684 else if (__builtin_expect (ch >= 0xff01, 1) \
4685 && __builtin_expect (ch <= 0xffe5, 1)) \
4686 cp = from_ucs4_extra[ch - 0xff01]; \
4687 else \
4688 { \
4689 UNICODE_TAG_HANDLER (ch, 4); \
4690 /* Illegal character. */ \
4691 cp = ""; \
4692 } \
4693 } \
4694 else \
4695 cp = from_ucs4_lat1[ch]; \
4696 \
4697 if (__builtin_expect (cp[0], '\1') == '\0' && ch != 0) \
4698 { \
4699 /* Illegal character. */ \
4700 STANDARD_TO_LOOP_ERR_HANDLER (4); \
4701 } \
4702 else \
4703 { \
4704 *outptr = cp[0]; \
4705 /* Now test for a possible second byte and write this if possible. */\
4706 if (cp[1] != '\0') \
4707 { \
4708 if (__glibc_unlikely (outptr + 1 >= outend)) \
4709 { \
4710 /* The result does not fit into the buffer. */ \
4711 result = __GCONV_FULL_OUTPUT; \
4712 break; \
4713 } \
4714 *++outptr = cp[1]; \
4715 } \
4716 ++outptr; \
4717 } \
4718 \
4719 inptr += 4; \
4720 }
4721#define LOOP_NEED_FLAGS
4722#include <iconv/loop.c>
4723

4726#include <iconv/skeleton.c>
